<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">

<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;2.02.</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following information is furnished pursuant to Item 2.02, &#8220;Results of Operations and Financial Condition,&#8221; and shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On June&#160;7, 2023, GameStop Corp. (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Company</span>&#8221;) issued a press release announcing its financial results for its first quarter ended April&#160;29, 2023. A copy of the press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The press release attached to this Current Report, including the exhibit, shall not be incorporated by reference into any filing of the Company, whether made before or after the date hereof, regardless of any general incorporation language in such filing, except as otherwise expressly set forth therein. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;5.02.</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Termination of President and Chief Executive Officer </span></p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On June&#160;5, 2023, the Board of Directors (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Board</span>&#8221;) of the Company terminated Matthew Furlong as President and Chief Executive Officer of the Company, effective immediately such that, after giving effect to such termination, Mr.&#160;Furlong was no longer employed by GameStop Texas Ltd., the Company, or any of their affiliates. Subject to Mr.&#160;Furlong&#8217;s timely execution of a Separation and Release Agreement (and <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-revocation</span> in the time provided to do so), which includes a release of claims against the Company and its affiliates, Mr.&#160;Furlong will be entitled to receive the payments and benefits associated with a termination without Cause, as such term is defined in Mr.&#160;Furlong&#8217;s offer letter dated June&#160;9, 2021 from GameStop Texas Ltd., which was originally filed as Exhibit 10.1 attached to the Company&#8217;s Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission on June&#160;9, 2021. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Board of Director Changes </span></p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On June&#160;5, 2023, Mr.&#160;Furlong resigned as a director of the Company, effective immediately. Mr.&#160;Furlong&#8217;s resignation did not result from any disagreement with the Company on any matter relating to the Company&#8217;s operations, policies or practices. In connection with Mr.&#160;Furlong&#8217;s resignation, the Board reduced the size of the Board to five. Additionally, as further disclosed in Item 8.01 to this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</span> the Board appointed Ryan Cohen as Executive Chairman of the Company and Alain Attal as the Lead Independent Director of the Board. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Appointment of General Manager </span></p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On June&#160;7, 2023, the Board appointed Mark H. Robinson as the Company&#8217;s General Manager, effective immediately. Additionally, Mr.&#160;Robinson was appointed as the Company&#8217;s principal executive officer. Mr.&#160;Robinson&#8217;s responsibilities will include administrative matters, corporate development, legal affairs and support for GameStop&#8217;s holdings, including the oversight of other executive officers besides the Executive Chairman, and he will report directly to Ryan Cohen, as Executive Chairman. Mr.&#160;Robinson will continue to serve in his roles as the General Counsel and Secretary of the Company. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mr.&#160;Robinson, 44 years old, has served as the Vice President, General Counsel of the Company since January 2022, and in various other roles at the Company since August 2015. In his current role, he oversees the legal and human resources functions of the Company.&#160;Prior to joining the Company in 2015, Mr.&#160;Robinson held positions as an attorney at law firms Norton Rose Fulbright and Jones Day, where he provided counsel on corporate and finance transactions. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In connection with his appointment as the General Manager, the Company and GameStop Texas, Ltd. entered into a letter agreement with Mr.&#160;Robinson on June&#160;7, 2023 (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Offer Letter</span>&#8221;) describing certain terms of his employment, which supersedes all prior agreements or offer letters between the parties regarding Mr.&#160;Robinson&#8217;s employment, unless otherwise noted therein. The Offer Letter provides that Mr.&#160;Robinson&#8217;s annualized salary will be $200,000 effective as of June&#160;7, 2023. The Offer Letter also provides that Mr.&#160;Robinson will continue to be eligible to receive the settlement of any transformation bonuses previously granted to him, and all equity and cash incentive awards previously granted to Mr.&#160;Robinson will continue to vest in accordance with their original terms, subject to Mr.&#160;Robinson&#8217;s continued employment with the Company and the satisfaction of any performance hurdles associated with those awards. The Offer Letter states that Mr.&#160;Robinson will be entitled to an additional grant of 9,300 restricted stock units of the Company&#8217;s Class&#160;A common stock, par value $0.001 per share, which award will vest in full on June&#160;12, 2024, subject to his continued employment through such date, as well as any other terms and conditions applicable to grant that are set forth in an individual award agreement to be entered into by Mr.&#160;Robinson and the Company on the grant date. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Under the Offer Letter, if Mr.&#160;Robinson&#8217;s employment is terminated without Cause (as defined in the Offer Letter), he will be entitled to receive the following severance benefits: (i)&#160;an amount equal to six months of his base salary, (ii)&#160;an amount equal to six months of COBRA premiums for Mr.&#160;Robinson and his eligible dependents, (iii)&#160;any transformation bonus installments which have not already been paid, (iv)&#160;the vesting of that portion of any equity award that was otherwise scheduled to vest in the ordinary course during the six month period immediately following his termination date, and (v)&#160;any long-term incentive cash award that was otherwise scheduled to vest in the ordinary course during the six month period immediately following his termination date. Mr.&#160;Robinson&#8217;s eligibility for these severance benefits is subject to his execution of a release of claims and his compliance with any applicable post-employment covenants. </p>
</div></div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>

There are no other arrangements between Mr.&#160;Robinson and any other person pursuant to which he was selected as an officer, nor are there any transactions to which the Company is or was a participant and in which Mr.&#160;Robinson has a material interest subject to disclosure under Item 404(a) of Regulation <span style="white-space:nowrap">S-K.</span> </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

Mr.&#160;Cohen&#8217;s responsibilities will include capital allocation, evaluating potential investments and acquisitions, and overseeing the managers of the Company&#8217;s holdings. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Additionally, on June&#160;7, 2023, the Board appointed Mr.&#160;Attal as the Lead Independent Director of the Board and dissolved the Strategic Planning and Capital Allocation Committee. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mr.&nbsp;Mark Robinson </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Dear Mark, </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Congratulations! I am pleased to offer you a
promotion to the role of General Manager of GameStop Corp. (the &#147;Company&#148;) effective as of today, which role you will assume in addition to your ongoing role as General Counsel and Secretary of the Company. You will continue to be subject
to all policies of the Company and GameStop Texas, Ltd. in effect from time to time, including the Company&#146;s Anti-hedging Policy, Clawback Policy, Insider Trading Policy and Code of Ethics. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Your new base salary will be at the annualized rate of $200,000 and will be effective as of June&nbsp;7, 2023. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">You will continue to be eligible to earn all transformation bonuses, restricted shares and stock units, and restricted long-term incentive cash in accordance
with, and subject to, the vesting and other terms of any award agreements that have been issued to you on or prior to the date hereof. For the avoidance of doubt, nothing in this letter shall change, eliminate or modify any terms of those award
agreements, certain terms of which are summarized below.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">A total of $396,000 in transformation bonuses are being paid <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">bi-weekly</FONT>
over the two year which began on July&nbsp;1, 2021. These bonuses are paid in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">bi-weekly</FONT> installments, as follows: In year 1, you received a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">bi-weekly</FONT> installment of
$<I>8,884.61</I>, less applicable taxes. In year 2, you have received (and for the remainder of year 2 you will remain eligible to receive) a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">bi-weekly</FONT> installment of $<I>6,346.15</I>, less applicable taxes.
Your right to receive each installment is conditioned on your continuous employment with us through the payment date of that installment<I>. </I>Except in case of your involuntary termination of employment without Cause as provided below, if your
employment with us ceases for any reason, no additional installments will be paid. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">On June&nbsp;9, 2020 you were granted two separate restricted long-term incentive cash awards, each in an amount
of $60,000 (for an aggregate amount of $120,000). <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Two-thirds</FONT> of each of these awards have previously vested and the last third of such awards will vest on the third anniversary of the grant date, subject to
your continuous service through such date and all required performance hurdles set forth within the individual award agreements. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">On May&nbsp;3, 2021, you were granted 2,284 restricted shares of the Company&#146;s Class&nbsp;A common stock
(&#147;Common Stock&#148;). The May 2021 equity award vests in equal installments on the first three anniversaries of the grant date, subject to your continuous service through the applicable vesting date. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="line-height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1.00pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">On July&nbsp;1, 2021 you were granted 11,632 restricted stock units of the Company&#146;s Common Stock. The July

2022 equity award will vest as follows: 16% on October&nbsp;1, 2022 and April&nbsp;1, 2023, and 17% on each of October&nbsp;1, 2023, April&nbsp;1, 2024, October&nbsp;1, 2024, and April&nbsp;1, 2025, subject in each case to your continuous service
through the applicable vesting date. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition to the above and in connection with your promotion, on June&nbsp;12, 2023, you will be
granted 9,300 restricted stock units based on the Company&#146;s Common Stock (the &#147;Additional Equity Award&#148;). The Additional Equity Award will fully vest on the one year anniversary of the date of grant, subject to your continuous service
through such date. The equity award referenced in this paragraph will be documented in a separate award agreement; that agreement will contain additional terms and conditions (not inconsistent with this letter) and be delivered to you following the
grant date, and the Additional Equity Award will be subject to all terms and conditions set forth in such award documentation. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company&#146;s
agreement to grant equity to you and to pay you transformation bonus installments does not guarantee your employment for any period or otherwise limit our ability to terminate your employment at any time, for any reason, even if your opportunity to
receive or vest in such equity or receive such signing bonus installments would be forfeited as a result of such termination. We will periodically review your performance and compensation levels and may make adjustments, all as determined in the
sole discretion of applicable management. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Consistent with all roles in the organization, your employment will remain on
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">an&nbsp;at-will&nbsp;basis,</FONT> having no specified term, and may be terminated at the will of either party on notice to the other. However, if we terminate your employment without Cause (as defined
on<U>&nbsp;Exhibit A</U>), you will receive the following severance benefits, subject to the conditions noted below: (i)&nbsp;we will pay you an amount equal to six months of your base salary, (ii)&nbsp;if you are participating in our group health
plans immediately prior to your termination, we will pay you an amount equal to the applicable premium for COBRA continuation coverage for you and your eligible dependents for six months, (iii)&nbsp;we will pay you any&nbsp;transformation&nbsp;bonus
installments which have not already been paid, (iv)&nbsp;the portion of any equity-based award that was otherwise scheduled to vest in the ordinary course during the six month period immediately following your termination date will become vested and
(v)&nbsp;any long-term incentive cash award that was otherwise scheduled to vest in the ordinary course during the six month period immediately following your termination date will become vested. To be eligible for these benefits you must
(x)&nbsp;sign a release of claims on such form as we supply (which form will be substantially consistent with that used for other terminating senior executives) and that release must become irrevocable within 60 days after your termination date, and
(y)&nbsp;comply with any applicable post-employment covenants under any other written agreement with us. The amounts described in clauses (i), (ii) and (iii)&nbsp;will be paid in a single cash lump sum (less required tax withholdings) as soon as
practicable after the release becomes effective, and in no event later than 70 days after the termination date. The shares described in clause (iv)&nbsp;will be issued (if not already outstanding) and released from transfer restrictions as soon as
practicable after the release becomes effective, and in no event later than 70 days after the termination date. The amount described in clause (v)&nbsp;will be paid in accordance with the terms of the Long-Term Incentive Cash Award Terms&nbsp;&amp;
Conditions and at the same time as all other participants in such long-term incentive cash program are paid. </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><U>Definition of Cause</U>. For purposes of the compensation letter, &#147;Cause&#148; mean any of the
following: (i)&nbsp;your conviction of, or plea of nolo contendere to, a felony or any crime involving fraud or dishonesty; (ii)&nbsp;your willful misconduct, whether or not in the course of service, that results (or that, if publicized, would be
reasonably likely to result) in material and demonstrable damage to the business or reputation of the Company or any of its affiliates or subsidiaries; (iii)&nbsp;material breach by you of any agreement with, policy of or duty owed to the Company or
any of its affiliates or subsidiaries; or (iv)&nbsp;your willful refusal to perform your duties to the Company or the lawful direction of your supervisor that is not the result of a disability; provided, however, an act or omission described in
clause (iii)&nbsp;or (iv) will only constitute &#147;Cause&#148; if (A)&nbsp;it is not curable, in the good faith sole discretion of the Company&#146;s Board of Directors (the &#147;Board&#148;) or its delegate, or (B)&nbsp;it is curable in the good
faith sole discretion of the Board or its delegate, but is not cured to the reasonable satisfaction of the Board or its delegate within 30 days following written notice thereof to you by the Company (such notice to state with specificity the nature
of the breach or willful refusal). However, a termination of your employment due to your death or Disability will not constitute a termination without Cause. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Disability&#148; means a written determination by a physician mutually agreeable to you and the Company (or, in the event of your total
physical or mental disability, your legal representative) that you are physically or mentally unable to perform your duties and that such disability can reasonably be expected to continue for a period of six consecutive months or for shorter periods
aggregating 180 days in any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">12-month</FONT> period. In addition, and without limiting the foregoing, a Disability shall be deemed to have occurred if you become entitled to receive benefits under any long-term
disability plan or policy maintained or funded by the Company. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><U>Compliance with Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;409A</U>. Section&nbsp;409A. The parties intend for all amounts
payable under this offer letter to be exempt from Section&nbsp;409A of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended (&#147;Section&nbsp;409A&#148;) and this offer letter will be interpreted accordingly. Nonetheless, the Company does not guaranty
the tax treatment of your compensation arrangements under Section&nbsp;409A or any other federal, state or local tax law. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g518333g0607194008171.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>GameStop Discloses First Quarter 2023 Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">GRAPEVINE, Texas&#151;(BUSINESS WIRE)&#151;June 7, 2023&#151;GameStop Corp. (NYSE: GME) (&#147;GameStop&#148; or the &#147;Company&#148;) today released
financial results for the first quarter ended April&nbsp;29, 2023. The Company&#146;s condensed and consolidated financial statements, including GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> results, are below. The Company&#146;s Form <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-Q</FONT> and supplemental information can be found at https://investor.gamestop.com. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>FIRST QUARTER OVERVIEW </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Net sales were $1.237&nbsp;billion for the period, compared to $1.378&nbsp;billion in the prior year&#146;s first
quarter. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Selling, general and administrative (&#147;SG&amp;A&#148;) expenses were $345.7&nbsp;million, or 27.9% of net
sales for the period, compared to $452.2&nbsp;million, or 32.8% of net sales, in the prior year&#146;s first quarter. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Net loss was $50.5&nbsp;million for the period, compared to a net loss of $157.9&nbsp;million for the prior
year&#146;s first quarter. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Transition costs related to European restructuring efforts were $14.5&nbsp;million for the period. For the second
quarter, the Company will continue to incur transition charges. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Cash, cash equivalents and marketable securities were $1.310&nbsp;billion at the close of the quarter.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Long-term debt remains limited to one <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-interest,</FONT> unsecured term loan
associated with the French government&#146;s response to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19.</FONT> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company will not be
holding a conference call today. Stockholders can review the Company&#146;s Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-Q.</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> MEASURES AND OTHER METRICS </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">As a supplement to the Company&#146;s financial results
presented in accordance with U.S. generally accepted accounting principles (&#147;GAAP&#148;), GameStop may use certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures, such as adjusted SG&amp;A expense, adjusted operating income (loss),
adjusted net income (loss), adjusted earnings (loss) per share, adjusted EBITDA and free cash flow. The Company believes these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provide useful information to investors in evaluating
the Company&#146;s core operating performance. Adjusted SG&amp;A expense, adjusted operating income (loss), adjusted net income (loss), adjusted earnings (loss) per share and adjusted EBITDA exclude the effect of items such as certain transformation
costs, asset impairments, severance, as well as divestiture costs. Free cash flow excludes capital expenditures otherwise included in net cash flows from (used in) operating activities. The Company&#146;s definition and calculation of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures may differ from that of other companies. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures should be viewed as supplementing, and not as an alternative or substitute
for, the Company&#146;s financial results prepared in accordance with GAAP. Certain of the items that may be excluded or included in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures may be significant items that could impact the
Company&#146;s financial position, results of operations or cash flows and should therefore be considered in assessing the Company&#146;s actual and future financial condition and performance. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

upon management&#146;s current beliefs, views, estimates and expectations, including as to the Company&#146;s industry, business strategy, goals and expectations concerning its market position, strategic and transformation initiatives, future
operations, margins, profitability, sales growth, capital expenditures, liquidity, capital resources, expansion of technology expertise, and other financial and operating information, including expectations as to future operating profit improvement.
Such statements include without limitation those about the Company&#146;s expectations for fiscal 2023, future financial and operating results, projections and other statements that are not historical facts. Forward-looking statements are subject to
significant risks and uncertainties and actual developments, business decisions, outcomes and results may differ materially from those reflected or described in the forward-looking statements. The following factors, among others, could cause actual
developments, business decisions, outcomes and results to differ materially from those reflected or described in the forward-looking statements: economic, social, and political conditions in the markets in which we operate; the competitive nature of
the Company&#146;s industry; the cyclicality of the video game industry; the Company&#146;s dependence on the timely delivery of new and innovative products from its vendors; the impact of technological advances in the video game industry and
related changes in consumer behavior on the Company&#146;s sales; interruptions to the Company&#146;s supply chain or the supply chain of our suppliers; the Company&#146;s dependence on sales during the holiday selling season; the Company&#146;s
ability to obtain favorable terms from its current and future suppliers and service providers; the Company&#146;s ability to anticipate, identify and react to trends in pop culture with regard to its sales of collectibles; the Company&#146;s ability
to maintain strong retail and ecommerce experiences for its customers; the Company&#146;s ability to keep pace with changing industry technology and consumer preferences; the Company&#146;s ability to manage its profitability and cost reduction
initiatives; turnover in senior management or the Company&#146;s ability to attract and retain qualified personnel; potential damage to the Company&#146;s reputation or customers&#146; perception of the Company; risks associated with new digital
asset products and services; the Company&#146;s ability to maintain the security or privacy of its customer, associate or Company information; occurrence of weather events, natural disasters, public health crises and other unexpected events;
potential failure or inadequacy of the Company&#146;s computerized systems; the ability of the Company&#146;s third party delivery services to deliver products to the Company&#146;s retail locations, fulfillment centers and consumers and changes in
the terms the Company has with such service providers; the ability and willingness of the Company&#146;s vendors to provide marketing and merchandising support at historical or anticipated levels; restrictions on the Company&#146;s ability to
purchase and sell <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-owned</FONT> products; the Company&#146;s ability to renew or enter into new leases on favorable terms; the potential monetary losses, user disputes, reputational harm and regulatory scrutiny
from any hacking, social engineering or other cyber attacks in connection with digital assets; the potential failure or inadequacy of the Company&#146;s or its third party partners&#146; systems or blockchain networks related to the Company&#146;s

Company&#146;s digital asset investments, products or services; potential exposure to litigation arising from violations of law by third parties using the Company&#146;s digital asset products or services; potential unfavorable development regarding
treatment of digital assets under U.S. and foreign tax laws; the Company&#146;s ability to comply with anti-money laundering and sanctions laws in connection with its digital asset products and services; volatility in the Company&#146;s stock price,
including volatility due to potential short squeezes; continued high degrees of media coverage by third parties; the availability and future sales of substantial amounts of the Company&#146;s Class&nbsp;A common stock; fluctuations in the
Company&#146;s results of operations from quarter to quarter; the restrictions contained in the agreement governing the Company&#146;s revolving credit facility; the Company&#146;s ability to generate sufficient cash flow to fund its operations; the

adjusted SG&amp;A expense, adjusted operating loss, adjusted net loss, adjusted EBITDA and adjusted loss per share. The diluted weighted-average shares outstanding used to calculate adjusted earnings per share may differ from GAAP weighted-average

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>GameStop Corp. </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Schedule III </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(in millions)
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(unaudited) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> results </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following table reconciles the Company&#146;s cash flows provided by operating activities
as presented in its unaudited Consolidated Statements of Cash Flows and prepared in accordance with GAAP to its free cash flow. Free cash flow is considered a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. Management believes,
however, that free cash flow, which measures our ability to generate additional cash from our business operations, is an important financial measure for use by investors in evaluating the company&#146;s financial performance. </P>

<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="right">(102.7</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">)&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">$</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="right">(303.9</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">)&nbsp;</TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:3.00em; text-indent:-1.00em; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Capital expenditures</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="right">(9.1</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">)&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="right">(10.8</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">)&nbsp;</TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="font-size:1px; ">
<TD VALIGN="bottom"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; border-top:1.00px solid #000000">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; border-top:1.00px solid #000000">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; border-top:1.00px solid #000000">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; border-top:1.00px solid #000000">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD>&nbsp;</TD></TR>
<TR BGCOLOR="#cceeff" STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1.00em; text-indent:-1.00em; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Free cash flow</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">$</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="right">(111.8</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">)&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">$</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="right">(314.7</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">)&nbsp;</TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="font-size:1px; ">
<TD VALIGN="bottom"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; border-top:3.00px double #000000">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; border-top:3.00px double #000000">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; border-top:3.00px double #000000">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; border-top:3.00px double #000000">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD>&nbsp;</TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Measures and Other Metrics </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted EBITDA, adjusted SG&amp;A expense, adjusted operating loss and adjusted net loss per share are supplemental financial measures of the Company&#146;s
performance that are not required by, or presented in accordance with, GAAP. We believe that the presentation of these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provide useful information to investors in assessing our
financial condition and results of operations. We define adjusted EBITDA as net income (loss) before income taxes, plus interest expense, net and depreciation and amortization, excluding stock-based compensation, certain transformation costs,
business divestitures, asset impairments, severance and other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> charges. Net income (loss) is the GAAP financial measure most directly comparable to adjusted EBITDA. Our
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures should not be considered as an alternative to the most directly comparable GAAP financial measure. Furthermore, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures
have limitations as an analytical tool because they exclude some but not all items that affect the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures. Some of these limitations include: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">certain items excluded from adjusted EBITDA are significant components in understanding and assessing a
company&#146;s financial performance, such as a company&#146;s cost of capital and tax structure; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">adjusted EBITDA does not reflect our cash expenditures or future requirements for capital expenditures or
contractual commitments; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">adjusted EBITDA does not reflect changes in, or cash requirements for, our working capital needs;
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">although depreciation and amortization are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> charges, the assets
being depreciated and amortized will often have to be replaced in the future, and adjusted EBITDA does not reflect any cash requirements for such replacements; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">our computations of adjusted EBITDA may not be comparable to other similarly titled measures of other companies.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We compensate for the limitations of adjusted EBITDA, adjusted SG&amp;A expense, adjusted operating loss, adjusted net loss and
adjusted loss per share as analytical tools by reviewing the comparable GAAP financial measure, understanding the differences between the GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures and incorporating these data
points into our decision-making process. Adjusted EBITDA, adjusted SG&amp;A expense, adjusted operating loss, adjusted net loss and adjusted net loss per share are provided in addition to, and not as an alternative to, the Company&#146;s financial
results prepared in accordance with GAAP, and should not be considered in isolation or as a substitute for analysis of our results as reported under GAAP. Because adjusted EBITDA, adjusted SG&amp;A expense, adjusted operating loss, adjusted net
income and adjusted earnings (loss) per share may be defined and determined differently by other companies in our industry, our definitions of these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures may not be comparable to
similarly titled measures of other companies, thereby diminishing their utility. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">10 </P>

</DIV></Center>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">GameStop Announces Election of Ryan Cohen as Executive Chairman </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">GRAPEVINE, Texas&#151;(BUSINESS WIRE)&#151;June&nbsp;7, 2023&#151;GameStop Corp. (NYSE: GME) (&#147;GameStop&#148; or the &#147;Company&#148;) today disclosed
that its Board of Directors has elected Ryan Cohen as Executive Chairman, effective immediately. Mr.&nbsp;Cohen&#146;s responsibilities include capital allocation and overseeing management. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In conjunction, the Company&#146;s former CEO has been terminated. </P>
